find ./memory/source_docs -type f \( -iname "*.pdf" -o -iname "*.pdf.gz" \) 2>/dev/null | sed 's|^\./||'

echo "=== PDF COUNT ==="
find ./memory/source_docs -type f \( -iname "*.pdf" -o -iname "*.pdf.gz" \) 2>/dev/null | wc -l

echo "=== DOCS MANIFEST (pdf/md/txt/docx/csv/json/yaml) ==="
printf "modified_at\tsize_bytes\tpath\n"
find . -type f \( -iname "*.pdf" -o -iname "*.md" -o -iname "*.txt" -o -iname "*.docx" -o -iname "*.csv" -o -iname "*.json" -o -iname "*.yaml" -o -iname "*.yml" \) \
  -not -path "./venv/*" -not -path "./.venv/*" -not -path "*/__pycache__/*" \
  -print0 | while IFS= read -r -d '' f; do
    sz=$(stat -f %z "$f")
    mt=$(stat -f "%Sm" -t "%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S" "$f")
    printf "%s\t%s\t%s\n" "$mt" "$sz" "$f"
  done | sort
